Home > Configuration Compare > Model Compare > Validate Response Returned From Successful Model Compare Request. > User compares the Options received from Configuration-Compare against the Options generated from Catalog-Options and Equipment Category.
  • Overall Test Results
  • Requirements
  • Themes
  • Capabilities
  • Features
Report generated 20-12-2019 14:00

Validate Response Returned From Successful Model Compare Request.

User submits a post request to the Configuration-compare service with x number of ccode's & Llp's.
The system verifies validates the request body and retrieves the Compare data for all models in the Request.
The User then verifies that response is Success, Validates the json Schema of the Response and
then verifies the data returned in the Response.
User compares the Options received from Configuration-Compare against the Options generated from Catalog-Options and Equipment Category.
 

Cast

 Mathew

  • Mathew can:
    • call an API at https://test2.chrysler.com/hostd/api

 actorInSpotlight

  • actorInSpotlight can:
    • call an API at https://test2.chrysler.com/hostd/api
  Steps Outcome
Given Mathew has a list of models to be Compared
codellpCode
CUJ202008KLJP74A2TG
SUCCESS 0s
And He has a stateCode for the Request
stateCode
LA
SUCCESS 0s
When He Makes a post request to configuration-Compare service with the Models and Ccode
SUCCESS 2.54s
Mathew post compare request
SUCCESS 2.53s
Mathew executes a POST on the resource /configuration-compare/compare
SUCCESS 2.53s
POST https://test2.chrysler.com/hostd/api/configuration-compare/compare

Response

Status code: 200

Content Type: application/json

Request Headers

Accept=*/*
Content-Type=application/json; charset=UTF-8

Content Body

{
    "models": [
        {
            "code": "CUJ202008KLJP74A",
            "llpCode": "2TG"
        }
    ],
    "stateCode": "LA"
}
